019533,003478:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
019534,003479: 
019535,003480:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
019536,003481:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
019537,003482:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
019538,003483:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
019539,003484: 
019540,003485:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019541,003486:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1) BY ENDIDLE
019542,003487:                                                                                                  #                2) BY NVSUBUSY
019543,003488:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
019544,003489:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019545,003490:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
019546,003491:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
019547,003492: 
019548,003493:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
019549,003494:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
019550,003495:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
019551,003496:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
019552,003497:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
019553,003498: 
019554,003499:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
019555,003500:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019556,003501:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
019557,003502:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019558,003503:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019559,003504: 
019560,003505:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
019561,003506:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
019562,003507:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
019563,003508: 
019564,003509: 
019565,003510:                                                                                                  #  .
019566,003511: 
019567,003512:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
019568,003513:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
019569,003514:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
019570,003515:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
019571,003516: 
019572,003517:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019573,003518:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
019574,003519:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
019575,003520:                                                                                                  #  1)    DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
019576,003521:                                                                                                  #        IS EXCEEDED.
019577,003522:                                                                                                  #  2)    CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 464 

019579,003524:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019580,003525: 
019581,003526:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
019582,003527:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
019583,003528:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
019584,003529:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
019585,003530:    4443           10647                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
019586,003531:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
019587,003532: 
019588,003533:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
019589,003534:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
019590,003535: 
019591,003536: 04,2647                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
019592,003537: 04,2647                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019593,003538: 04,2647           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
019594,003539: 04,2650           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019595,003540: 04,2651           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
019596,003541: 04,2652           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
019597,003542: 04,2653           30001                           CA       L                                     
019598,003543: 04,2654           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
019599,003544: 04,2655           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019600,003545: 
019601,003546:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
019602,003547:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
019603,003548:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
019604,003549:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
019605,003550:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
019606,003551: 
019607,003552:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
019608,003553:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019609,003554:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019610,003555:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
019611,003556:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019612,003557:    4450           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
019613,003558:    4451           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
019614,003559:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019615,003560:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
019616,003561:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
019617,003562:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
019618,003563:    4455           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2. PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
019619,003564:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
019620,003565: 
019621,003566:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
019622,003567:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
019623,003568:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
019624,003569:

019627,003572:    4461           44736                           CS       BIT14

019769,003714:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
019770,003715:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
019771,003716:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
019772,003717:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
019773,003718:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
019774,003719:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
019775,003720:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
019776,003721:

019780,003725: 40,3604           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #  LIGHT RESET LEAVES DSPLOCK UNCHANGED.
